of&nbsp;</span><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/page/1283483/ec2vc\" target=\"_blank\"><span>EC2VC</span> Investors Forum and Pitch Competition</a> with <span>45+ of the most active professionals.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/page/1290885/patients-20\" target=\"_blank\"><span>NEW in 2017: Patients 2.0 Forum</span> -&nbsp;</a><span>a 3-hours interactive height: 31px;\"></a></p>\n<p>In 2017 we're excited to be a co-located partner with <a href=\"http://www.healthio-global.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\">HEALTHIO</a>, a new trade show event with a fresh and interactive approach for health professionals, patients and other stakeholders to experience the latest innovations in healthcare. HEALTHIO brings together decision-makers in the healthcare sector to share their experience and knowledge in clinical innovation and its impact on healthcare management.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Trade show activities will include product demonstrations, workshops, talks, debates, knowledge acceleration areas and other activities combined to create a genuinely interactive experience. HEALTHIO will be co-located with Health 2.0 Europe May 3-5 at Fira Montjuic, Plaza Espaa. You can learn more about HEALTHIO <a href=\"http://www.healthio-global.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>.</p>\n<p><span class=\"fr-video fr-dvb fr-draggable\"><iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/Y4l_CQLAVeo\" allowfullscreen=\"\" width=\"425\" height=\"225\"></iframe></span></p>\n                    </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\" margin-bottom-medium col-xs-12 col-sm-6 \">\n                    <div class=\"col-xs-12 trade-template\">\n                        <p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"fr-dib fr-draggable\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/bizzabo.users.files/nQZj0tPQVqqpwJfqx0ij_image.png\" style=\"width: 212px; height: 73.4933px;\"><br><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><strong><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/agenda/session/163721\" target=\"_blank\">EU eHealth Competition</a>&nbsp;</strong></span></p> \n<p>The 6th eHealth Competition will be held in Barcelona on May 3rd in partnership with Health 2.0 Europe and Healthio.<br><br>The eHealth Competition is an initiative that rewards the best eHealth/ mHealth solutions produced by SMEs. Its objective is to support business success of SMEs by giving them visibility together with marketing opportunities to attract customers, partners and external capital.<br><br>The 6th Edition call for applications will remain open until the 28th February. The novelty this year is the launch of a Diabetes track to reward the best solutions for the population management of the disease. This track is linked to the ProEmpower initiative (Pre-commercial Procurement). Companies that reach the final phase will receive up to 1,140,000 . <a href=\"https://events.bizzabo.com/H2conEurope2017/agenda/session/163721\" target=\"_blank\">Learn more</a> and <a href=\"https://www.ehealthcompetition.eu/registration/\" target=\"_blank\">Register now!&nbsp;</a></p>\n                    </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\" margin-bottom-medium col-xs-12 col-sm-6 hide\">\n                    <div class=\"col-xs-12 trade-template\">\n                        <p>Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetuer adipiscing elit. Moderated by Roberto Ascione, CEO of Healthware International (Italy), EC2VC is a pitch competition and networking opportunity with the most active European investors in digital health!&nbsp;</p>\n<p>12 finalists will be invited to make a 4-minute pitch presentation followed by 4 minutes of Q&amp;A with our jury panelists. The jury panelists will select 2 winners in 2 categories: <strong>Early stage funding</strong> (revenues under 250K/year) &amp; <strong>Series A</strong> (revenues over 250K/year)</p>\n<p>For more information including applications to pitch, agenda, and investor judges visit the <a href=\"https://events.bizzabo.com/H2conEurope2017/page/1283483/ec2vc\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>EC2VC page</strong></a>.<br><br></p>\n<hr>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><br><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/page/1290884/doctors-20\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>Doctors 2.0</strong></a></span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>in partnership with:</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"fr-dib fr-draggable\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/bizzabo.users.files/XRMgES9JRDWQtuwu21pV_Screen%20Shot%202017-03-06%20at%209.08.24%20PM.png\" style=\"width: 300px;\"></p>\n<p>Doctors 2.0 brings together health professional pioneers to share their experiences with each other, and features the latest tools, applications, and programs for physician collaboration, workflow and enhancing the patient-provider relationship by engaging patients with their care. <a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/page/1290884/doctors-20\" target=\"_blank\">Read more</a>.</p>\n                    </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\" margin-bottom-medium col-xs-12 col-sm-6 \">\n                    <div class=\"col-xs-12 trade-template\">\n                        <p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-draggable\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/bizzabo.users.files/XV1DV9mMQn6C73ZtIiKr_eHealth%20Hub%20Logo.png\" style=\"width: 124px; height: 82.1192px;\"></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/agenda/session/163718\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>Investment Readiness Academy</strong></a>&nbsp;</span></p>\n<p>Thinking of raising money? Technology has supported the rising of their voices: they became increasingly informed and empowered, they called for a redefinition of the doctor/patient relationship, they started using new tools to co-produce their own health, became actors of their own care, and they are now getting increasingly involved in the co-design of these Health 2.0 solutions and giving a new sense to the words \"patient-centricity\". <span style=\"font-size: 14px;\">This session is <strong>FREE</strong> to everyone.&nbsp;</span><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/page/1290885/patients-20\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-size: 14px;\">Read more</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 14px;\">.</span></p>\n<p><br></p>\n                    </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\" margin-bottom-medium col-xs-12 col-sm-6 hide\">\n                    <div class=\"col-xs-12 trade-template\">\n                        <p style=\"text-align: center;\"><br><img class=\"fr-dib fr-draggable\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/bizzabo.users.files/nQZj0tPQVqqpwJfqx0ij_image.png\" style=\"width: 212px; height: 73.4933px;\"><br><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><strong><a href=\"https://europe2017.health2con.com/agenda/session/163721\" target=\"_blank\">EU eHealth SME Competition</a>&nbsp;</strong></span></p> \n<p>The eHealth Competition is an initiative that rewards the best eHealth/ mHealth solutions produced by SMEs.
